<userid>105271558116109845798<//userid><name>J. Kevin Mann<//name><Date>1522328613787< /Date><Rating>4< /Rating>< Review>
The food is good quality, but the experience is a little chaotic, reflecting a busy restaurant and not quite enough seating at busy times.  When your food is ready, they call out your number and you have to retrieve your food from the counter.  When you are done, you need to bus your own dishes.  So, overall, this is organized as a fast-food restaurant, although the food is healthier and better quality than we usually associate with fast food.  It's a bit out of the way for our family, but we still go occasionally since everyone likes the food.  I try to avoid the busiest times, since the crowding can detract from the experience.<//Review>

We love Cactus! They have everything we want here, crunchy or soft, small or large, vegetarian or meaty, savory or sweet... YUM! Kid-friendly, seat yourself, order and pickup at the counter. 103241442684350147772< /userid>
< review>
Cactus is my favorite choice to go for excellent Mexican food in North Berkeley. They have a variety of tasty food options ranging from tacos to enchiladas to soup.

My wife and I love the grilled chicken plate which comes with guacamole, beans, cheese, rice, fresh salsa, lettuce and three warm corn tortillas. Be sure to try  on of their delicious fresh agua frescas with your meal.

They do get busy at meals times so I highly recommend calling your order in if you are planning to get take out. The staff is friendly and helpful so don't forget to tip when you are at the register.< /review>

< Review>
Great swim school with great teachers. Prior to Sutton, my daughter was going to Flying Fish in Mountain View but due to scheduling conflicts, we had to look for a new swim class and I'm glad I found Sutton.

The facility is very clean and well maintained. The staff are very friendly and helpful. Their scheduling is more flexible than other places. What I like about it is that it's an on-going enrollment. So once you enroll in a class for a certain time and day, you're good to go. At Flying Fish, you had to re-enroll every term and there were no guarantees that you will be able to enroll in something that matches your preference (which is why we decided not to continue with them).

They offer private, semi-private and group. Their price for semi-private was very reasonable for us so we went that route. Her teacher (Ms. Krista) is AMAZING! She knows how to deal with little kids and make sure they enjoy their time with her. When Ms. Krista is not available, we have had a very good experience with the substitute teachers. So overall, I think all the teachers are good.

They are very organized. I like their check-in process. Their evaluation, testing and overall pool policy is very organized and I like that.

The pool is clean and very warm. They have plenty of showers. The parents viewing window is also nice.

They have a kids area in the parents viewing where kids can watch cartoon and have their after-swim snacks.

I'm also very happy with my daughter's progress.

I highly recommend the swim school.<//Review>

My staple movie house. Covid smart. Big and clean, everyone helpful, any lines go quick. Been going for about 4 years now, not a complaint yet.<//Review>

< user_id>
100832189033931876976</user_id>
<GmapID>0x80d95712c182eb2b:0x3f9305d08c408ba7</GmapID><name>Scott Heavill< /name>< response>

</record></dataset><record>
<Response>None< /Response><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
Freshly popped popcorn, highly carbonated cola, and Titan surround sound. What a blast! Watching a new espionage action film was a "Wow" experience. Movies.. at the movies is an ultimate leisure activity.

Reading Cinema has excelled safety protocols.
First, still cheap. Only $8.50 a ticket. Seat reservations still exist but with 3 seats in between same row and no one behind it in front of you. All contactless. Not even your tickets are touched. Entrance through the theater, exit into the mall. This eliminates crowd contact and crowd crossing. No more self-serve but employee service assisted.

I am thrilled and hope you can support this family pastime. No cash accepted.
Credit/debit cards.

4< /rating>
< text>
Finding a theater that has comfortable seating, a good selection of films, and cost less than $9 for a normal ticket is, in my experience, unusual for San Diego so I highly recommend Reading Cinema in the Grossmont Mall center.

I went to see Black Panther the Friday it was released and the cinema had enough showings that I could find one that was only half full instead of packed. Yet it also has smaller films available on a regular basis.

I would give it 4.5 Stars if I could and the only reason I'm not giving it 5 Stars wholly is because they will run films for only 1 or 2 weeks if they feel they aren't being successful enough. That makes it difficult to plan on a trip with multiple people to a smaller film or even a larger film like Annihilation that isn't getting a lot of ticket sales at this location.< /text>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
I've been coming to the theater at Grossmont since I was a baby. The first movie I remember seeing was Mouse Hunt (1997). That put me at about 3 years old. The theater is my favorite place to be. The name has changed a few times through the years. Reading Cinemas gave it a much needed makeover. The concessions menu is much better. I like the bacon grilled cheese. The ticket prices are the most reasonable in town at $8.50. Even the Titan XD which I try to watch as much as I can. I really like that it's 360 surround sound. The best thing about Reading Cinemas is they allow outside food. I often grab Coldstone before I watch my movie. The staff is always super friendly and helpful. The auditoriums are cleaned properly after every showing. On Sunday's you can get a large popcorn, two medium drinks and candy for $10. Large popcorns are refillable. It's a very pleasant place to be.</Text>
